SQL> 
SQL> -- --------------------------------------------------------
SQL> --  Step #1
SQL> --  -------
SQL> --  Using the query from Lab 7, Step 4, insert the 135
SQL> --  rows in the PRICE table created in Lab 6.
SQL> -- --------------------------------------------------------
SQL> 
SQL> -- Insert step #1 statements here.
SQL> SET PAGESIZE 99
SQL> SELECT   DISTINCT c.contact_id
  2  FROM     member m INNER JOIN transaction_upload tu
  3  ON       m.account_number = tu.account_number INNER JOIN contact c
  4  ON       m.member_id = c.member_id
  5  WHERE    c.first_name = tu.first_name
  6  AND      NVL(c.middle_name,'x') = NVL(tu.middle_name,'x')
  7  AND      c.last_name = tu.last_name
  8  ORDER BY c.contact_id;

SQL> 
SQL> 
SQL> SET NULL '<Null>'
SQL> COLUMN rental_id	     FORMAT 9999 HEADING "Rental|ID #"
SQL> COLUMN customer	     FORMAT 9999 HEADING "Customer|ID #"
SQL> COLUMN check_out_date   FORMAT A9	 HEADING "Check Out|Date"
SQL> COLUMN return_date      FORMAT A10  HEADING "Return|Date"
SQL> COLUMN created_by	     FORMAT 9999 HEADING "Created|By"
SQL> COLUMN creation_date    FORMAT A10  HEADING "Creation|Date"
SQL> COLUMN last_updated_by  FORMAT 9999 HEADING "Last|Update|By"
SQL> COLUMN last_update_date FORMAT A10  HEADING "Last|Updated"
SQL> SELECT   DISTINCT
  2  	      r.rental_id
  3  ,	      c.contact_id
  4  ,	      tu.check_out_date AS check_out_date
  5  ,	      tu.return_date AS return_date
  6  ,	      3 AS created_by
  7  ,	      TRUNC(SYSDATE) AS creation_date
  8  ,	      3 AS last_updated_by
  9  ,	      TRUNC(SYSDATE) AS last_update_date
 10  FROM     member m INNER JOIN transaction_upload tu
 11  ON       m.account_number = tu.account_number INNER JOIN contact c
 12  ON       m.member_id = c.member_id
 13  LEFT JOIN rental r
 14  ON c.contact_id = r.customer_id
 15  AND trunc(tu.check_out_date) = TRUNC(r.check_out_date)
 16  AND TRUNC(tu.return_date) = TRUNC(r.return_date)
 17  WHERE    c.first_name = tu.first_name
 18  AND      NVL(c.middle_name,'x') = NVL(tu.middle_name,'x')
 19  AND      c.last_name = tu.last_name
 20  ORDER BY c.contact_id;

SQL> INSERT INTO rental
  2  SELECT NVL(r.rental_id,rental_s1.NEXTVAL) AS rental_id
  3  ,	    r.contact_id
  4  ,	    r.check_out_date
  5  ,	    r.return_date
  6  ,	    r.created_by
  7  ,	    r.creation_date
  8  ,	    r.last_updated_by
  9  ,	    r.last_update_date
 10  FROM (SELECT DISTINCT
 11  		  r.rental_id
 12  	   ,	  c.contact_id
 13  	   ,	  TRUNC(tu.check_out_date) AS check_out_date
 14  	   ,	  TRUNC(tu.return_date) AS return_date
 15  	   ,	  1001 AS created_by
 16  	   ,	  TRUNC(SYSDATE) AS creation_date
 17  	   ,	  1001 AS last_updated_by
 18  	   ,	  TRUNC(SYSDATE) AS last_update_date
 19  	   FROM member m INNER JOIN contact c
 20  	   ON	m.member_id = c.member_id INNER JOIN transaction_upload tu
 21  	   ON	c.first_name = tu.first_name
 22  	   AND	NVL(c.middle_name,'x') = NVL(tu.middle_name,'x')
 23  	   AND	c.last_name = tu.last_name
 24  	   AND	tu.account_number = m.account_number LEFT JOIN rental r
 25  	   ON	c.contact_id = r.customer_id
 26  	   AND	TRUNC(tu.check_out_date) = TRUNC(r.check_out_date)
 27  	   AND	TRUNC(tu.return_date) = TRUNC(r.return_date)) r;

4681 rows created.

SQL> -- --------------------------------------------------------
SQL> --  Step #2
SQL> --  -------
SQL> --  Add a NOT NULL constraint on the PRICE_TYPE column
SQL> --  of the PRICE table.
SQL> -- --------------------------------------------------------
SQL> 
SQL> -- Insert step #2 statements here.
SQL> 
SQL> SET NULL '<Null>'
SQL> COLUMN rental_id	     FORMAT 9999 HEADING "Rental|ID #"
SQL> COLUMN customer	     FORMAT 9999 HEADING "Customer|ID #"
SQL> COLUMN check_out_date   FORMAT A9	 HEADING "Check Out|Date"
SQL> COLUMN return_date      FORMAT A10  HEADING "Return|Date"
SQL> COLUMN created_by	     FORMAT 9999 HEADING "Created|By"
SQL> COLUMN creation_date    FORMAT A10  HEADING "Creation|Date"
SQL> COLUMN last_updated_by  FORMAT 9999 HEADING "Last|Update|By"
SQL> COLUMN last_update_date FORMAT A10  HEADING "Last|Updated"
SQL> SELECT   DISTINCT
  2  	      r.rental_id
  3  ,	      c.contact_id
  4  ,	      tu.check_out_date AS check_out_date
  5  ,	      tu.return_date AS return_date
  6  ,	      3 AS created_by
  7  ,	      TRUNC(SYSDATE) AS creation_date
  8  ,	      3 AS last_updated_by
  9  ,	      TRUNC(SYSDATE) AS last_update_date
 10  FROM     member m INNER JOIN transaction_upload tu
 11  ON       m.account_number = tu.account_number INNER JOIN contact c
 12  ON       m.member_id = c.member_id
 13  LEFT JOIN rental r
 14  ON c.contact_id = r.customer_id
 15  AND TRUNC(tu.check_out_date) = TRUNC(r.check_out_date)
 16  AND TRUNC(tu.return_date) = TRUNC(r.return_date)
 17  INNER JOIN common_lookup cl
 18  ON      cl.common_lookup_table = 'RENTAL_ITEM'
 19  AND     cl.common_lookup_column = 'RENTAL_ITEM_TYPE'
 20  AND     cl.common_lookup_type = tu.rental_item_type
 21  LEFT JOIN rental_item ri
 22  ON r.rental_id = ri.rental_id;

SQL> INSERT INTO rental_item
  2  SELECT rental_item_s1.NEXTVAL AS rental_item_id
  3  , r.rental_id
  4  ,	    r.item_id
  5  ,	    r.created_by
  6  ,	    r.creation_date
  7  ,	    r.last_updated_by
  8  ,	    r.last_update_date
  9  ,	    r.rental_item_price
 10  ,	    r.rental_item_type
 11  FROM    (SELECT   r.rental_id
 12  	      ,        tu.item_id
 13  	      ,        TRUNC(r.return_date) - TRUNC(r.check_out_date) AS rental_item_price
 14  	      ,        cl.common_lookup_id AS rental_item_type
 15  	      ,        1001 AS created_by
 16  	      ,        TRUNC(SYSDATE) AS creation_date
 17  	      ,        1001 AS last_updated_by
 18  	      ,        TRUNC(SYSDATE) AS last_update_date
 19  	      FROM member m INNER JOIN contact c
 20  	   ON	m.member_id = c.member_id INNER JOIN transaction_upload tu
 21  	   ON	c.first_name = tu.first_name
 22  	   AND	NVL(c.middle_name,'x') = NVL(tu.middle_name,'x')
 23  	   AND	c.last_name = tu.last_name
 24  	   AND	tu.account_number = m.account_number INNER JOIN common_lookup cl
 25  	     ON cl.common_lookup_type = tu.rental_item_type
 26  	     AND cl.common_lookup_column = 'RENTAL_ITEM_TYPE'
 27  	     AND cl.common_lookup_table = 'RENTAL_ITEM' LEFT JOIN rental r
 28  	   ON	c.contact_id = r.customer_id
 29  	   AND	TRUNC(tu.check_out_date) = TRUNC(r.check_out_date)
 30  	   AND	TRUNC(tu.return_date) = TRUNC(r.return_date)) r ;

11520 rows created.

SQL> -- --------------------------------------------------------
SQL> --  Step #3
SQL> --  -------
SQL> --  Update the RENTAL_ITEM_PRICE column with valid price
SQL> --  values in the RENTAL_ITEM table.
SQL> -- --------------------------------------------------------
SQL> 
SQL> -- Insert step #3 statements here.
SQL> 
SQL> INSERT INTO transaction
  2  SELECT NVL(r.transaction_id,transaction_s1.NEXTVAL) AS transaction_id
  3  ,	    r.transaction_account
  4  ,	    r.transaction_type
  5  ,	    r.transaction_date
  6  ,	    r.transaction_amount
  7  ,	    r.rental_id
  8  ,	    r.payment_method_type
  9  ,	    r.payment_account_number
 10  ,	    r.created_by
 11  ,	    r.creation_date
 12  ,	    r.last_updated_by
 13  ,	    r.last_update_date
 14  FROM (SELECT t.transaction_id AS transaction_id
 15  	   ,	  tu.account_number AS transaction_account
 16  	   ,	  cl1.common_lookup_id AS transaction_type
 17  	   ,	  TRUNC(tu.transaction_date) AS transaction_date
 18   --     ,	    SUM(tu.transaction_amount) OVER (PARTITION BY r.rental_id) AS transaction_amount
 19  	   ,	  SUM(tu.transaction_amount / 1.06) AS transaction_amount
 20  	   ,	  r.rental_id
 21  	   ,	  cl2.common_lookup_id AS payment_method_type
 22  	   ,	  tu.payment_account_number
 23  	   ,	  1001 AS created_by
 24  	   ,	  TRUNC(SYSDATE) AS creation_date
 25  	   ,	  1001 AS last_updated_by
 26  	   ,	  TRUNC(SYSDATE) AS last_update_date
 27  	   FROM member m INNER JOIN contact c
 28  	   ON	m.member_id = c.member_id INNER JOIN transaction_upload tu
 29  	   ON	c.first_name = tu.first_name
 30  	   AND	NVL(c.middle_name,'x') = NVL(tu.middle_name,'x')
 31  	   AND	c.last_name = tu.last_name
 32  	   AND	tu.account_number = m.account_number INNER JOIN rental r
 33  	   ON	c.contact_id = r.customer_id
 34  	   AND	TRUNC(tu.check_out_date) = TRUNC(r.check_out_date)
 35  	   AND	TRUNC(tu.return_date) = TRUNC(r.return_date)INNER JOIN common_lookup cl1
 36  ON      cl1.common_lookup_table = 'TRANSACTION'
 37  AND     cl1.common_lookup_column = 'TRANSACTION_TYPE'
 38  AND     cl1.common_lookup_type = tu.transaction_type INNER JOIN common_lookup cl2
 39  ON      cl2.common_lookup_table = 'TRANSACTION'
 40  AND     cl2.common_lookup_column = 'PAYMENT_METHOD_TYPE'
 41  AND     cl2.common_lookup_type = tu.payment_method_type LEFT JOIN transaction t
 42  ON t.TRANSACTION_ACCOUNT = tu.payment_account_number
 43  AND t.TRANSACTION_TYPE = cl1.common_lookup_id
 44  AND t.TRANSACTION_DATE = tu.transaction_date
 45  AND t.TRANSACTION_AMOUNT = tu.TRANSACTION_AMOUNT
 46  AND t.PAYMENT_METHOD_type = cl2.common_lookup_id
 47  AND t.PAYMENT_ACCOUNT_NUMBER = tu.payment_account_number
 48  GROUP BY t.transaction_id, tu.account_number, cl1.common_lookup_id, tu.transaction_date,
 49  r.rental_id, cl2.common_lookup_id, tu.payment_account_number) r;

4681 rows created.
